! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------


! At the moment, these continuation lexica are identical. But since I
! suspect that linguistic input will prove that the words behave
! differently, they are kept distinct.

! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON VNAME ! Names ending in stressless vowel
 N_OTHERS ;


LEXICON NYSTØ ! Names ending in stressed vowel, typically scand. compounds 
 N_OTHERS ; ! check whether this is correct!


LEXICON SNAME ! Southern Sami names
 N_OTHERS ;

! Consonant-filal names
! - - - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON CNAME
 +N+Sg+Nom:0 FINAL1 ; ! The bare nominative, of unassimilated names
 :e N_OTHERS ; ! making C-final names into vowel stems


! The lexica
! ==========

LEXICON ProperNoun

! Southern Sami names (to be alphabetized when we have a stable lexicon)
! ----------------------------------------------------------------------

Jense SNAME ;
Karijuse SNAME ;
Baktuse SNAME ;

! Some Sami family names

Kappfjell CNAME ;
Bransfjell CNAME ;
Fjellheim CNAME ;
Dunfjell CNAME ;
